---I. 8. Who bad shown his power with regard to the work aimed at by Indra, who bad proved his capacity to do the work intended

---I. 10. सोहं 'I therefore,' 'hence I.'

---II. 12-13. Said by Kautsa when he found that Raghu had made Kubera pour down treasure from the heavens. वृत्ते स्थितस्य him who acts according tothe duty (right policy)\' of kings. मनी\_\_ &c., 'even the heaven has been made to yield your desired object. '

---II. 16-17. ज्येष्ठा 'the eldest daughter of Himavat.' त्रिपथ\_\_ 'running in three streams,' through Heaven, Earth, and Patala.

---1. 20. राज्याश्रममुनिं 'the king who was, as it were, a Muni in the hermitage in the form of a kingdom.'

P. 26. 1. 2. काकपक्षधरं 'who wore (graceful) side-locks of \_\_\_ i.e. who was quite a boy; a Gen. Tat. compound. तेजसां &c. 'as is not considered in the case of those who are possessed of lustre of Bhartrihari 'न खलु वयस्तेजसो हेतुः'.

---1. 3. कृपयाविष्टं 'overcome by (the feeling of) pity'.

---11. 5-8. The Sarat season is here compared to a clever messenger who takes her friend (the Ganges) to her lord (the ocean) in a perfectly pleased mood (with its extremely pure waters) after having, with great difficulty, brought her to the right path (having brought the river to its usual course), who has grown lean (which has shrunk within its bed), and who was much enraged at her husband's having many wives (which had turbid water in the rain the ocean too, having several wives, the rivers).

---II. 9-12. मम वचनात् 'at my instance, in my name'. पूर्वाभा\_\_ &c. 'This (कुशलप्रश्न) is the only mode of address (to be used) by those beings who are easily subject to miseries'.

---11. 13-18. सः 'Rama'. याचमानः शिवं सुरान् 'begging a blessing of the gods', praying to gods to wish well of Sita., यथास्थितं सर्वं 'every--

283

thing as it stood'. भिश्नमाणो वनं प्रियां 'asking the forest (any information about) his beloved'. 1. 21. 'As if, \_\_\_\_\_ out life from himself, he confined sorrow to his mind', i.e. became very desperate and hence was sad at heart. 1. 17 throws out a, conjecture. आ is a particle meaning'yes, perhaps it may be'.

LESSON V.

P. 32. 1. 4. अनांययत्, i.e. हारीतः, when he found the little parrot in that helpless state. मुक्तप्रयत्नं 'who had left off struggling.'

---1. 7. येन &c. 'By whom my friend was made to rely on that person false to his promise'.

---1. 9. आसनं प्रतिग्राहितः 'you were made to carry the (Guru's)seat.'

---1. 10. धात्रीकर्मवस्तुतः परिगृह्य 'having taken charge (of them) commencing with the duty of a nurse,\' i.e. doing all that a nurse would have done under the same circumstances. Perhaps the sentence may be read as धात्रीकर्म वस्तुतः परिगृह्य 'having actually undertaken a nurse's duties'. वृत्तचूडौ after the tonsure ceremony was over.' त्रयीवर्जं 'excepting the three Vedas.'

---1. 16. Said by Chandrapida to Sukanasa, when requesting him to persuade his father to allow him to go to bring back Vaisampayana.

---1. 18.-19. They two, having lamented, made the killer of their child extract from his heart the dart therein implanted'.

P. 33. 11 2-3. सांगं 'with its angas, which are six: Siksha, Chhandas, Vyakarana, Nirukta, Kalpa and Jyotisha'. उत्कांतशैशवौ who had passed their (state of) childhood.' कविप्रथमपद्धतिं 'the first pathor road of (to be followed by) poets,' who first showed poets the way. He is 'आद्यः कविः' and hence the epithet.

---1. 8. भावेन 'by your honour', referring the Sutradhara.

---1L 13-14. Said by Rati to Cupid after he had been reduced

284

to ashes by Siva रजनी\... मार्गे may be simply locative, or locative absolute. Enveloped in nocturnal darkness.'

P. 33, 11. 15-16. तां कुलप्रतिष्ठां प्रणमय्य--'making her, who was the glory or strength (source of stability) of the family, bow down to the tutelary deities. कारयितव्यदक्षा 'knowing well what others should be made to do'. सतीनां पादग्रहणमकारयत् 'made her seize (fall at) the feet of the chaste (matronly) women'.

---1. 17. एकोन्मीलनपेशलः 'Calculated to at once unfold (recall to memory).'

---11. 19-20. उत्सवसंकेतान्--name of a people. जयोदाहरणं 'declaration or announcement of his victory' i.e. verses declaratory of the success of his arms.

---1. 21. अथ 'after the death of Dasaratha.' अनाथाः 'without a lord' owing to the king's death,'

---11. 23-24. Said by Rama to Sita रक्षसा 'by Ravana.'

---1. 25.---P. 34. 1. 2. Said by Draupadi to Yudhishtira. 'What other king than yourself, who has all means favourable to him and who is proud of his family, will allow others to take away his wealth like his own wife, attached to him by virtue of good qualities, and born of a noble family', क इव 'who possibly.'

P. 34.II 3-6. These four lines and the next two are addressed by Ravana to Sita, when he was endeavouring to win over her mind to himself. यः etc. 'he who extracts milk from a stone, will alone derive happiness from Rama', meaning that it is simply impossible. बोधयंतं हिताहितं 'who (Ravana) is telling you what is good and bad.' किं विलापयसे 'why make me talk much'.

---11. 7-8. 'Employ the demons and myself in rendering your service.' 1. 25. 'who will not wish for the reverential bow made by Indra by folding his hands on his head,' i.e. as Indra, my conquered vassal, bows down to me, so will he bow down to you, my dear beloved. मूर्धानमधिगतः, or अधिगतो मूर्धा येन तमधिमूर्धानं.

285

P. 34. 11. 9-10. एनं i.e. रामं रक्षोगणं क्षिप्नुं 'calculated to disperse (destroy) the multitude of demons.' गाधिसुतः Visvamitra.

LESSON VI.

P. 38. 1. 24. अधरोत्तरव्यक्तिर्भविष्यति 'it will be manifest; who is inferior and who is superior.'

---11. 26-27. अहं--अयः Canadasa, who complained to the king about Haradatta.

P. 39. 1. 1. 'I conjure you by the life of' &c. if you do not say it in words. Said by Madhava, when Malati simply nodded replies to his questions.

---11. 10-11. जरद्रद्रविडधार्मिकः 'an old Dravida ascetic.' इच्छया goes with निसृष्टैः and means 'to the satisfaction of.' अभिमतं goes with मनोरथः 'wished for,' 'cherished.'

---1. 14. किं बहुना 'why say much,' to be brief.

1 17. 'I am ashamed of my very heart, now that it knows the whole affair.'

P. 40. 11. 1-2. जनस्य scil. अस्ति 'belongs to,' 'is possessed by'. 1. 21 'Then garden-creepers are, indeed, distanced, by wild creepers in point of excellence,' i.e. 'nature unadorned adorns the most'.

---11. 3-4. Describe the state of Sudakshina when pregnant. असमग्रभूषणा 'not having put on all her ornaments,' but only a few necessary ones, such as मंगलसूत्र, कंकण &c. मुखेन=मुखेनोपलक्षिताः तनुप्रकाश 'of dim lustre'. विचेयतारका the night 'the stars in which have to be searched out,' being very few, as it is nearly day-break.

---1. 6. मर्त्येषु असंमूढः 'he, among all men, who, undeluded, knows me' etc.

---1. 10. अकथ्यमाने i.e. पुण्डरीकवृत्तांते.

---11.16-17. Translate: 'Proud women, though they, having first slighted a prostration, are subsequently stung with remorse, are

286

nevertheless secretly (at heart) ashamed of propitiating their beloved ones, i.e. do not like to openly conciliate them.

P. 40.11. 18-19. Said by Rama to Sita, -when Lakshmana said 'यावदार्याया हुताशने विशुद्धिं' till the purification of Sita by fire.' Rama means to say: 'Pity it is that people have to be propitiated by those whose wealth consists in their noble (untarnished) family, and hence that step (purification) was taken simply to please the people; and therefore what ill we have said of you, does not indeed befit you.' न=अस्माभिः.

---11. 20-21. Every instrumental is to be construed with the noun following it. अविनयबहुलतया etc.'because blooming youth abounds, in. immodest acts.' तमपि=पुण्डरीकं.

---1. 24---P. 41. 1.2. स्पृशति पदं 'attains to a position.' गुण etc. 'being connected with (arising from) the possession of a number of qualities', which are not found in the dog.

P. 41. 1. 3. इति=मयि.

---1. 5. विनयप्रधानैः--विनयः प्रधानः येषां 'amongst which modesty stands foremost'.

---11. 12-15. नंदमौर्यनृपयोः goes with अस्तोदयौ अविभिन्नकालं simultaneously'. These lines show the superiority of Chanakya to the sun: 'Who surpasses, by his lustre, the lustre of the thousand-rayed god, which is not all-pervading, and which causes cold and heat in alternate succession, (and hot at one and the same time as did Chanakya).

---11. 20 21. Describe the qualities of Duryodhana. उद्यतं 'uplifted' or drawn against enemies. His orders are most respectfully obeyed by kings. गुण also means 'a thread'.

---11. 24-25. Refer to Sisupala, as described by Narada to Vishnu. बालः 'while yet a boy'. मुखेन etc. 'in face, being like the full moon, he was like the three-eyed god.' 1. 20 'Now he, being a youth (grown-up man), who has made kings subject to tributes, is, to be

287

sure, pre-eminently like the sun (who occupies the mountains with his rays).'

LESSON VII.

P. 47. 1. 20. सर्वज्ञस्य the sense of the instrumental. 'Undertaking to decide by only one person, howsoever omniscient, is liable to be faulty'.

---1. 23. अस्मै scil. बालकाय.

---1. 25. साधोः 'given to a good person.'

P. 48. I. 1. Said by Ganga to Earth when she was angry with Rama for having abandoned her daughter, Sita. शरीरमसि संसारस्य 'you are the very body (main stay) of worldly life.

---11.3-4. मिथ्या\... निर्भरः 'full of pride of pretended (false) greatness.' आत्मप्रज्ञा etc. 'they hate the minister's advice thinking that it (following the advice) is degrading (derogatory to) their own wisdom'.

---1. 6. महाश्वेताप्रणामपुरःसरं 'first making his salutation (paying his respects) to Mahasveta'.

---1. 9. अवाङ्मनसगोचरं 'who is beyond the reach (range) of speech and mind', i.e. who can neither be described nor conceived.

---11. 10-11. An address to the moon. The Amavasya (new moon day) occurs when the moon enters (आवसति) the body of the sun but for which, there being no Darsa day, there would be no performance of sacred rites by the pious. सुधया &c. cf. पर्यायपीतस्य सुरैर्हिमांशोः कलाक्षय श्लाध्यततो हि वृद्धो (R. V. 16.), the waning of the moon from day to day being ascribed to his being drunk up, digit by digit, by the Gods and Manes.

---11. 12-13. Said by the seven sages to Himalaya when they asked Uma in marriage for Siva. त्वत्वुल etc. 'this manner (collection of circumstances) is sufficient to elevate your family'.

288

P. 48. 11. 14-15. तृणबिन्देः परिशंकितः 'Indra afraid of Trinabindu' who was practising austere penance. Gods, and especially Indra, are always afraid of the penance of others; of Sakuntala Act I. -- 'अस्त्येदन्यसमाधिभीरुत्वं'. हरिणी name of a nymph.

---11 18-19. Said by Kautsa, when be found Raghu almost penniless, and wished to take his departure. निर्गलिरांबुगर्भं etc. 'even the Chataka does not trouble (press with request) an autumnal cloud, whose watery contents have been poured out or emptied.'

---11. 20-21. 'The king having approached that only son (of his parents) who was in that condition, told them both his deed done through ignorance.' उपेत्य, according to some means उद्दिश्य.

P. 49. 1. 4.\* 'falling quite prostrate on the ground,' like a stick lying horizontally down.

---1. 6. रामस्य दर्शनं सुहृदां 'the seeing of friends by Rama; Rama's seeing his friends.'

---1. 8 कुलपांशव 'a disgrace to the family' who sully the honour of their family.

---11. 12-13. स=दिलीपः. यज्ञाय 'for the performance of sacrifices which keep gods contented. Indra sent down rain (lit. milked the heaven) for corn to grow; thus they two reciprocated services and supported the two worlds. गां दुदोह 'milked the earth' (took taxes).

---11. 14-15. An address to Brahman. केवलात्मन् 'who was single, undivided.' गुणत्रय---'Rajas, Satva, and Tamas.' Brahma was afterwards divided at the time of creation, the three qualities appearing respectively at the times of creation, preservation, and destruction.

---1. 16. दुःखात्सुखमुपनतं 'that happiness which falls to one's lot after (suffering) misery,' the savouriness of the pleasure arising from contrasted enjoyment.

---1. 24. अरुणाय कल्पते 'is fit to receive Aruna' the harbinger of the sun, which indicates the close of night.

P. 50.1. 2. अनुहुंकुरुते 'roars in return.'

289

P. 50. 11. 3-4. तथेति saying 'yes'. संतानकामाय \'who longed for issue or progeny'.

---11. 5-0. तस्याः goes with प्रसादं\... 1. 6. 'Communicated to his beloved the favour of the cow, inferred from the signs of delight (on his face), in words which were, as it were, superfluous, as the very appearance of delight, informed the queen of the auspicious event.

---11. 9-10. पुराणशोभां &c. 'restored to its former grandeur or magnificence.' न स्पृहयांबभूव etc. 'did not at all envy the happiness of either, because he already enjoyed it in his capital.'

---1. 12. सानुनीतिः=सानुनयः 'assuming a conciliatory tone.'

---11. 13-16. दिदृक्षुं--त्वं शुभा न वेति द्रष्टुमिच्छन्तं. 1.14. 'It is the very character of demons that they should make inquiries about others wives. नमुस्कुर्याः scil. यदि.

LESSON VIII.

P. 56. I. 1. सत्क्रियाविशेषात् 'on account of the distinguished reception' (on the part of Indra); the king means to say that he has done nothing to merit such a grand reception at Indra's hands.

---1. 9. सूर्योपस्थानात् प्रतिनिवृत्तं 'returned after having served, or waited upon, the sun'.

---1. 18. उज्जिहानजीविता 'whose life is departing, or leaving her.'

---1. 20. उत्तरोत्तरं 'more following more', 'talking more and more.'

P. 57. 1. 1. तासां=अप्सरसां.

---11. 5-6. Said by Pururavas to the swan. तावत् 'first,' 'before doing anything else.' 1. 6. 'To the good the business' of a supplicant is more weighty (important) than their own interest'.

---11. 7-8. तपसे कृतोद्यमां 'who had made up her mind to practise penance.' मुनिव्रतं=तपश्चरणरूपं.

290

P. 57.1. 10. तदभावे &c.---In its absence (there being no protection) even that which exists becomes non-existing, i.e. there is no security of person or property.

---II. 11-12.स=रघुः. अस्त्रं 'the science of missiles.' His father himself was his guru.

---11. 13-14. तस्मात् 'from the conqueror, Raghu.' आत्मा संरक्षितः 'the Suhmas saved themselves.' वैतसीं वृत्तिमाश्रित्य 'following the course of reeds\', which bend down to the current of water; hence, 'yielding to a stronger enemy.'

---11. 19-20. Describe the position of 'Madhyadesa.'

P. 58, II. 2-3. जन्मकर्मतो मलिनतरजनं 'the people in which were dirtier than their birth and deeds.' निर्घृणतर etc. 'all whose practices were more abominable than their hearts.'

---11. 4-5. She considers the pleasure garden to be the bow of Cupid, which is lovely on account of having arrows made of flowers, and the garden is, also lovely on account of bees clinging to the flowers. शिलीमुख 'arrow,' and 'bee.' पीतरक्ताः--पीताश्च ते रक्ताश्च, Champaka and Asoka being yellow and red respectively; and \* when taken with रजनिचर.

---1. 6. आत्मसंपद् 'self-excellence.' अभिजनात्प्रभृति 'beginning with noble descent.'

---I. 13. लब्धप्रसरा 'who has got room for free or unhampered conduct,' 'grown ascendant.' दुःखोपचर्या 'served or propitiated with difficulty'.

---1. 16. विनयाधानं 'imparting moral training,' 'teaching good manners'.

---11. 18-19. नवः=अजः; नवेतरः=रघुः. 1. 19. 'He, of firm resolve, did not desist from his practice of meditation till he had seen the Supreme Being.'

---1. 22. स्वनुष्ठित 'well-observed.'

291

P. 58.II 26-29. Said by Sita, -when she found Maruti near her in the Asoka garden. पूर्वस्मात् &c. 'he appears to be different from the former (i.e. Ravana), since he devoutly glorifies Rama; or is it that he has come here to inspire confidence in me, without any cruelty? प्रभातात् प्राक् scil. दृष्टानि स्वप्नदर्शनादीनि शुभनिमित्तानि.

---1. 30. P. 59. 1. 3. स=मारुतिः; तां=सीतां. प्रीतेः पराजयमानां 'who found (Ravana's) addresses to be unbearable.'

P. 59. 11. 6-7. एकाक्षरं 'the one syllable' ओम्. सावित्र्यास्तु परं नास्ति 'there is nothing superior to Savitri,' the celebrated Gayatri Mantra (which has to be silently repeated or muttered).

LESSON IX.

P. 64. 1. 6. वर्तमानकवि 'a living or contemporary poet'.

---1. 10. बद्धभाव 'has fixed her affection' on you. इतोगतं=स्वयि आहितं.

---1L 11-12. Said by Lava to Kusa.

P. 65. 1. 5. संसर्गमुक्तिः खलेषु=खलसंसर्गभुक्तिः, 'shunning the company of wicked people.'

---1. 7. संतानार्थाय विधये 'for (the performance of) some rite having for its object progeny.'

---11.12-13. Said by Indra to Cupid, when entrusting to him a great mission. आत्मसमं 'you who are like myself;' भूधरतामवेक्ष्य 'seeing his capacity to hold up the earth.'

---1. 15. कृत्स्नं गोत्रमंगलं 'Sita who formed the entire auspiciousness of both the families.

---11.19-20. ईशं 'their lord.' i.e. Rama. नितांत &c. 'who entertained a very cruel thought with respect to Sita,\' i.e. of abandoning her.

---11. 21-22. परकर्मापहः 'destroying the works of his enemies.'1.22. 'Striking his foes in their weak points, he covered his own weak ones.'

292

P. 65. 11; 23-27. Said by Rakshasa to Lakshmi with reference to the want of appreciation of merits shown by her in leaving Nanda and falling in love with Cliandragupta.

P. (HI. 11. 1-3. Said to Vidushaka by Dushyanta who was pleased with the picture of Sakuntala, though he had himself first repudiated her when she came to him in person.

---11. 9-10. Said by Ravana to Sita, when she contemptuously spurned all his supplications. प्रतिपत्तिपराङ्मुखी 'not inclined to acknowledge me' as your lord.

---11. 13-14. स=जनकः. आप्तवचनात् 'from the words of the trustworthy sage.' At these words of the sage, Janaka became assured of the manly heroism existing in Raghava though he appeared to be but a boy.' त्रिदशगोपमात्रके 'of the size of an Indragopa insect,' as small as etc.

LESSON X.

P. 75. 1. 23. विश्रंभातिशयप्रसंगसाक्षिणः 'bearing testimony to the occurrences (incidents) of much familiarity' between us two.

P. 76. 1. 1. एवमवस्थिते 'under these circumstances.'

---1. 2. तत्र प्रभवति देवी 'your ladyship has lull power to do that' etc.

---11. 5-6. अयं जमः i.e. Malati. न खलु etc. 'that being is surely not dead, who is remembered by his beloved.'

---1.13. समरशिरसि 'in the front of battle,' 'in the thickest of the fight.'

---11. 16-18 सर्वदेवमयस्य 'he was like Narayana, who represents all gods, because he had the several deities dwelling in himself. 'Dharma in the mind. i.e. he was as straightforward or righteous as Dharma, etc.

---11. 15-20. Certainly Dharma staying here in his entirety, setting at naught the sports of Kali age (being not influenced by its

293

effects) does not think of the (good old) Krita age,' the age proper for Dharma; so good is the life of those who dwell in this hermitage.

P. 76. 1, 22. तव प्रसादस्य etc. 'but with you, the blessings have preceded your favour', against the general course of cause and effect.

P. 77. 1. 2. शीर्षच्छेद्यः 'to be decapitated.' ते=त्वया.

---11.3 4. अकामयेतां scil. \* two mothers, Kausalya and Sumitra.

---11. 5-6. Said by Sita to Lakshmana, when she was ruthlessly abandoned. मद्वचनात् 'in my name.'

---1. 7. द्वादशः परिवत्सरः 'it is now 12 years since the World was made destitute of the queen,'

---1. 9. मैथिल्यभिज्ञानं=मैथिलि अभिज्ञानं

---H. 12-13. सा=सीता. 'Knowing the entry of the monkey into the (impregnable) city Lanka to be a miraculous occurrence'.

---11 15-18. Reflections of Sita, at her first seeing Maruti alighting in the garden. She first believes him to be Ravana. 11. 17-18 state why she does not believe that the person had been sent by Rama. 'Dwelling to the north of this sea, how could Rama know this city situated to the south of the salt ocean?'

LESSON XI.

P. 82. 1. 1. Said by Parivrdjika, when she was told to sit as a judge to decide the quarrel between the two dancing preceptors. \* etc.---a question; 'is a jewel examined in a village there being a town (hard by)', meaning the king alone was fit to do the duty asked of her.

---1. 3. मा तावत् 'oh, do not do so\', 'hold, hold.'

---1. 5. किं दीपिकापौनरुक्त्येन 'why the super fluity of lights' 'why want these lights', they are superfluous.

294

P. 82.1. 7. किं वृत्तं \'what became of her', 'how it fared with her.'

---1. 8. रघुकदंबकेषु 'the pre-eminent among Raghus'.

P. 83,1. 4.स्मर्तव्यशेषं नयामि 'make him only remain in memory', i.e. kill him.

---11. 7-8. बीजं Sita herself, who, when she was pregnant, was cast off.

---11. 9-10. सा Prithvi. मा मात व्याहरत्येव 'just as he (the lord) was saying 'oh, do not, do not take her away'.

---1. 18. पतनाय वल्लरी 'a creeper (dependent on the tree)tends (is sure) to fall down'.

---11. 21-22. The strong minded are not deterred by the appearance of danger.

P. 84.1. 1. संतानवाहीनि 'continuously flowing', 'incessantly working.'

---I 2. स्रोतः सहस्रैरिव संप्लवन्ते 'flow together, as it were, in thousands of currents,' find out thousands of new channels to vent themselves.

---1. 3. पञ्चभिः 'the five constituent elements.' पञ्चत्वं गते 'reduced to the state of five', resolved or decomposed into its component members.

---11. 7-8. तस्मिन्=अस्त्रे the missile which was used by Kusa against Vasuki to get back his golden bracelet. समाविद्ध etc. 'with its hands in the form of waves tossed about through agitation.' रोधांसि निघ्नन् 'violently dashing against the sides'.

---11. 11-14. Rakshasa says to Malayaketu that everything is ready for action, and every circumstance is favourable to them. त्वद्वाच्छांतरितानि 'obstructed by your desire,' i.e. 'only desire to march onward and everything else is ready.' The several locative absolutes show the favourable cironmstances. चलिताधिकारविमुखे 'indifferent, being dismissed from his authority.' मार्ग etc.---योग is superfluous; 'whose business is only pointing out the way'.

295

P. 84.11. 15-18. Said by Asvatthaman, 1. 15. Who acted like -the submarine fire in the ocean consisting of the enemy's forces lapped by the flames of the missiles hurled against them.

LESSON XII.

P. 90. 11. 20-23. The four lines give the use of all the short forms in the sense of the instrumental; 'fit to be served by you or us.'

---1. 26. कार्यवशात् 'for my purpose', that I might understand and realise the events of that time.

P. 91.11. 1-2. Said by Sita जातनिर्विशेषाः 'just like my children.'

---1. 3. वाग्विषयीभूतः 'who formed the subject of our talk.'

---1. 10. संदिशन्ति 'send love-messages'. समुपसर्पन्ति 'draw near their beloved ones.'

---11. 12-13. एकः--अपरः Aja and Raghu.प्रभुशक्तिसंपदा 'by the excellence of his sovereign power'. प्रभुशक्ति consisting of कोष, दण्ड and बल. प्रणिधानयोग्यया 'by the practice of concentration (meditation)'. शरीरगोचरात् 'visible (existing) in (pervading) the body.'

---11. 14-15. Krishna says to Arjuna: 'Those who are deprived of their discerning power by various desires, look up to other gods, performing various rites and controlled (guided) by their own nature.'

---11. 18-19. Describe the state of those who are puffed np with the possession of riches. व्यसनशत &c. 'though become the mark of hundreds of calamities', though exposed to hundreds of miseries, they do not perceive that their fall is imminent like that of the drops of water on the ends of grass growing on ant-hills.

---I. 20. मणिदर्पणमिव etc.---on account of its lucid and transparent water, it served, as it were, as a mirror for the Goddess of Splendour to see her face in.

296

P. 92.11. 1-2. नरपतिः the Chedi king. आविश्चकार 'put forth', 'exhibited.'

---1. 5. अर्थोष्मणा विरहितः 'devoid of the warmth of wealth'; cf. the English phrase 'a warm man.'

I.18. 'As is seen in Chitra and the moon in their conjunction when freed from mists.\'

II.19-20. The peculiarity of a slanderer is that he poisons the ears of one and destroys another (by reason of his backbiting), unlike the ordinary course of bites, which kill only him who is bitten.

---11. 21-22. Describe the qualities of Aja. 1. 22. 'The prince die not differ from his (generating) cause, his father, just as a lamp lighted from another, does not differ from it' (in flame or light).

LESSON XIII.

P. 97. 1. 12. ते गतिं ज्ञास्यन् 'wishing to know your fate,' what had become of you.

---1. 14. वारितप्रसरः 'prevented from advancing.'

---11. 16-17. श्रुतमृषेः 'learnt from the sage', of which he had heard from the sage. 1. 17. Raghava became excited though he was no conscious of the acts of his former existence (in the Dwarf incarnation).

---11.20---21. Said by Mahasveta, when her mind was drawn by Cupid towards the holy sage Pundarika.

P. 98. 1. 16. कथकेशिकेन्द्रः=भोजः, the king of the Vaidarbhas. चन्द्रं &c. 'like the sea, with its surging waves, going to meet the moon', which occurs at the phenomenon known as Tides.

---1. 7. अवश्यकर्तव्ययतामापतितं has become such as must be done', has become an imperative necessity.

---1. 8. दक्षिणाक्षि &c. 'should be made to take the hint given by the contraction (winking) of the right eye'; you should wink at them in such a manner that they will at once understand what you mean.

---1. 5. 'A heart, agitated by grief, is eased (disburdened) only by lamentations.'

---11. 10-11. हसितं मुदा प्रसितं 'laughter delightfully continued.' विलसितं etc. 'joyous sports, enlivened by love' decreased. \* 'destitute of exhilerating passions.' पुरहितं etc. 'and what was beneficial to, and desired by, the town was not done.'

---11: 12-16. Said by Kanva, when sending Dushyanta a message. संयमधनान् 'whose only wealth is their restraint of passions.' कथमप्यचांधवकृतां 'not in any way brought about by her relatives.' 11. 15-16 'She should be looked upon by you as one of your wives with a respect common to all. Further than this rests with fate; it should not be uttered (referred to) by the relatives of the bride.'

'How' says he, 'did it not occur to his mind that he, who even now served his master's cause though they themselves were dead and gone, would not certainly ally himself with his professed enemies, so long as he lived safe and sound?'

LESSON XVI.

P. 117.1. 29. नौ गुणदोषतः परिच्छेत्तुं 'to examine or test us with regard to our merits and demerits,' so as to ascertain our excellences and defects.

---1. 6. का गणना 'what need we say of,\' 'much more is it true in the case of.'

---11. 8-9. अचिराधिष्ठितराज्यः 'who has newly acquired sovereignty,' whose sovereignty is newly established. अरूढमूलत्वात् 'not having struck deep roots in (the minds of) his subjects,' and who, therefore, resembles a tree which is loose on account of its being newly planted (when it has not struck its roots deep in the soil).

300

what was there which was not calculated to enchant the hearer\'s mind?'

P.119.1. 4. अनुभवसमां वेदनां 'an agony equal to that when (they are) experienced', i.e. the same grief as that when the miseries are actually suffered. स्मरण etc. 'Be, therefore, pleased, not to make your life the fuel (prey) of the fire of sorrow caused by the recollection (of past incidents).

---11. 9-10. Said sarcastically by Bhima.

---11. 11-14. वेगोदग्रं 'deadly by reason of its quickness of circulation,' 'deadly in its effect.' अयं भरः 'this pre-eminence or superiority' exists in them naturally (जात्या).

11.15-16. Said by Siva disguised as an ascetic. बहुक्षमा 'possessed of much patience.

---11. 23-26. यसौ 'the twins' i.e. Nakula and Sahadeva कथैव नास्ति 'no account need be taken of' विस्फुरित etc. 'who has drawn (made to vibrate) his circular bow' (or perhaps his bow and wheel).

LESSON XXIII.

P. 168. 1. 21. भर्तृगतया 'about her husband'. गतया=संचन्धिन्या.

--- 1. 11. Said by Parvati to her friend. स्पुरितोत्तराधरः=स्फुरणभूयिष्ठः अधरो यस्य सः 'whose lip was greatly throbbing,' making a movement to speak; or better still 'whose upper and lower lips were throbbing'.

---11. 19-20. परोक्षमन्मथः 'who has had no percept nor experience of love', who is put of the reach of the influence of love. 1. 20. 'Let not, O friend, that (which was simply uttered in jest,) be taken in earnest'.

P. 170. 11. 6-7. Said by Sarngarava to Dushyanta when he said he could not believe Sakuntala's words. शाठ्यमशिक्षितः 'untrained to guile'. अप्रमाणं 'is not (regarded as) an authority', 'is not held trustworthy.' विद्या इति 'considering it to be a regular branch of learning'.

---II. 8-9. त्वं यस्य नेत्रतोः पथि स्थिता 'in whose range of sight you stood' by chance, and whose eyes, therefore, became अवंध्य (not useless, having reaped their fruit). रुढसौहृदः 'of deep-rooted friendship'.

---11. 10-11. Said by Himalaya to the seven illustrious sages. रजसोपि परं 'even higher than (transcending) the Rajas quality'.

---11. 12-13. Raghu's father was not only the sole Emperor, but also the sole (unrivalled) archer in the land.

---11. 14-15. सूखश्रव 'pleasant to hear'. दिवौकसां पथि आकाशे.

306

P. 170.11. 18-19. अन्यथावृत्ति \'changed', 'perturbed'. कण्ठाश्लेषप्रणतिनि longing for a close embrace of the neck'.

---1, 22. अशिक्षितपटुत्वं 'untaught guile or cunning'.

---11. 26-27. Agnimitra means to say that the severe pangs caused by Cupid seem hardly consistent with his weapon which is apparently so harmless, being only made of flowers; therefore the saying that 'the softer it is, the harder (to bear)\', is realised in Cupid.

---11. 28-29. ॰दर्शनाश्वासि 'derives encouragement or consoles itself by seeing the manifestations of her love'. रतिं etc. 'the desire of both of us produces satisfaction', the very idea that we love each other contributes to make me happy.

P 182. 1. 31. ज्ञानवृद्धभावः 'being advanced (grown old) in Knowledge,' i.e. 'though both equally learned.' पुरस्कारमर्हति 'is entitled to precedence.'

Ramabhadra instead of Maharaja यथाभ्यस्त 'as is your wont,' you are accustomed to do'.

---11. 15-18. आत्तदन्डः 'having assumed the sceptre.' अतनुषु etc. There may be kinsmen in affluent circumstances (when there are abundant means of income), but in you is summed up (comprehended the whole duty of a kinsman towards your subjects,' i.e. there may be found many parasitical gluttons in days of prosperity, but yon are the real kinsman of the people in good as well as bad days.

---11. 19-20. करणोज्झितेन 'forsaken by the senses' of perception, touch etc., i.e. grown senseless. तैलनुनिषेकबिन्दुना with the drop of dripping oil.'

---11. 21-22. कान्तिप्रदः 'giver of lustre' मासो etc., 'the month of Vaisakha,' spring-time, when the trees are laden with flowers.

LESSON XXVII.

P. 194. 11. 3-4. अभिनिवेश्य 'directing(the mind) to objects.' कालान्तरक्षमो न भवति 'is unable to brook delay.'

---11. 14-15. ईदृशः etc. 'such has turned out to be the lot (fate) if your being created.'

---11. 18-19. The meaning is that, the more the desire for wealth is cherished, the more it leads one to commit dark deeds. The simile is taken from a lamp, which gives out more and more soot as the same is made brighter and brighter.

P. 195. 1. 4. भस्मावशेषं चकार 'reduced to ashes'.

---11. 5-6. Just as the Ganges is revered for having taken its rise from the foot of the Supreme Being (Vishnu), so also is it revered for having derived its second source from your high head. Said with reference to the Himalaya mountain personified. उच्छिरसा whose head (speaks) has gone up into the sky.

---II. 11-12. अभिषेकान्ते 'at the conclusion of the coronation ceremony'.1. 12. By which their own sacrifices, with complete gifts, would be completed,' i.e. wealth sufficient to enable them to complete their sacrifices.

---11 14-15. विरलजनसंपाते 'frequented by a few people.' विमानोत्संग same of the king's palace.

P. 196. I. 1. लोकयात्रा सिद्धा \'thiscourseoflife is settled '

---1. 11. Since transitoriness first claps to the bosom one that is born, and then the mother like a nurse, what ground is there for amentation?'

---11. 15-16. उभयोः=कुशलवयोः; 'the people wondered not so much it their skill in music as at their thorough disregard to the freewill gifts offered by the king'.

310

P. 196.1. 20. A salutary advice to those who are in the habit doing things at the eleventh hour.

LESSON XXVIII.

P. 201. 11. 9-10. Said by Sukanasa to Chandrapida सुखं विशा \'easily find access to.'

---11. 11-12. सर्वतोमुखी 'in every respect,' 'unlimited,' 'complete'.

---11. 13. यस्य refers to Himalaya.

---11. 16-17.The idea of the lines is best expressed by 'Unity is strength.'

P. 202. 11. 7-8. Said by Chandrapida's mother to Manorama the time of allowing him to go to bring back Vaisampayana.

---11. 9-10. असंशयं etc. scil. शकुन्तला. 1- 10. The meaning is thatthe secret prompting (the inner voice) of the heart of good men is a same guide for them to follow, since it can never think of an illegitimate object.

---11.11-14. Said by Dushyanta to Sakuntala. एवंप्राया etc. For such for the most part, is the behaviour of those, over whom darkness (of infatuation) exercises mastery, in auspicious (good) matter (on auspicious occasions).

---11. 15-19. एवमादिभिः i.e. उपायैः. सा=उर्वशी. तदाश्रयिणी 'relating to her.'

---11. 20-21. 'They call you who are immovable (another Vishnu, for your belly (interior) (like Vishnu's) has become the support of beings, movable and immovable.'

---11. 22-25. Describe the position in which the cloud messenger will probably find the Yaksha's wife. भावगम्यं 'conceived by the mind'.

P. 203.1. 3. मखजं 'caused by the great Visvajit sacrifice,' in which Raghu had given away all his wealth.

311

P. 203. 11. 5-6. इयं Malavika. प्रेष्यभावेन 'in the capacity of a servant.' वा 'like'

---11 7-8. पंक्तिरथः=दशरथः, पंक्ति meaning '10'. What Dasaratha, transgressing the rules, did, was, indeed, forbidden to the king; (how, then, did he, a wise king, do it?) for even learned persons, when blinded by (the quality of) darkness (passion) set foot on the wrong road.'

---11. 20-23. Said by Rakshasa when he found the plot most cleverly laid against him by the wily Chanakya. शकटेन=शकटदासेन his bosom friend.

---11. 28-29. Said by Agnimitra when he found it difficult to conceal any longer from Iravati his ardent love for Malavika. खंडनहेतवः 'occasions or pretexts to disappoint her\'.

---1. 29. 'But not a form of courtesy (polite behaviour) towards proud or intelligent women, though (it be) greater than before, but wanting in sincerity.'

LESSON XXIX.

P. 211. 11. 18-19. शक्ति 'regal power which has three constituent elements: प्रभाव 'the majesty or pre-eminence of the king himself'; मंत्र 'the power of good counsel', and उत्साह 'the force of energy'.

---11. 22-23. 'Oh! the property of those who are bereft of support through the failure of issue (lineal descendants) passes over to another, at the decease of the original progenitor (from whom in a direct line the family is descended).

P. 212. 11. 6-7. These lines refer to Vishnu. कल्पान्तदुःस्था 'being in a distressed state at the end of the Kalpa (the time of general deluge).' ऊहे 'was uplifted or drawn out'.

---11. 9-10. परः 'enemy.' 1. 10. 'For he (an enemy) and a disease, when growing, are regarded by the wise, as the same' (in

312

their fatal effects). i.e. if their growth be not checked in time, they will prove very injurious.

P. 212.11. 11-12. Said by the bards to Aja, at the time of announcing to him the time of rising'. त्वत्प्रबोधप्रयुक्तां 'employed to rouse you from sleep.\'

---1. 15. सर्वतोमुखं 'having faces in all directions', because he was चतुर्मुख.

---II. 17-18. स=हिमालय. पितॄणां मानसीं कन्यां 'the girl was a mental creation of the Fathers'(created by virtue of their desire, and not by the ordinary means).

---1. 19. नव इव चिरेणापि 'my grief is, as it were, new, although so many (12) years have since then elapsed.

P. 213. 1. 3. असौ Hanumat

---II. 6-7. The Jumna and the Ganges, having respectively black and white waters, seem to provide for each other black aloe and sandal ointment.

---1. 9. स्फुटन्निव etc. 'as if bursting out on account of the flood (excess) of internal excitement.\'

---II. 10-11. वयो etc. 'the resemblance between Rama and the two (Lava and Kusa) differing only in age and dress\' i.e. they two and Rama resembled in every respect except age and dress. नाक्षिकंपं व्यतिष्ठत 'stood, without the twinkling of their eyes\', stood fixing upon them a steadfast gaze.

---1. 14. मरुतः सुतं Bhima. दर्शितविक्रियं 'who had shown a change in mind', emotion of anger.

---11. 18-19. तद्योधाः 'his warriors\'. 1. 19 'On grounds covered over with excellent bides of antelopes and surrounded by vines.'

---1. 20 श्रुतमधिगम्य 'having acquired a sound knowledge'. शरीर\_ जन्मनः रिपून् Desire, Anger, Avarice etc., the six passions.

---1. 21. 'They soon bring upon Wealth the stigma (.i\'l-repute)

313

of unsteadiness,' i.e. wealth leaves such persons and becomes habit?to be called चपला.

P. 213.11.22-25. प्रियप्राया 'for the most part kind. 1. 25 'the flavour (interest) of which is unchanged (unabated) either before or afterwards,' i.e. which is at all times equally pleasing.

---1. 27. न संस्थास्यते 'will not stop,\' will be accomplished.

---11. 28-29. सीतां obj. of द्रष्टुं. उपाक्रंस्त 'proceeded towards the sea-shore.'

P. 214. 11.1-2. The past participles are used as abstract nouns.

1\. 2.Lanka(with so many jumbled noises)produced a noise resembling that in the city of Indra'.

---11. 3-4. The son of the Wind was for a time pleased at the sight of Ravana of whom, being afraid, the thousand-eyed (Indra) ceased from fight.'

---11. 5-6. यावदर्थपदां 'having words just enough to convey the meaning,' not using many words.

---1. 7. अखिलीकृत्य 'without having made powerless.'

---11. 9-12. मोपयध्वं भयं 'do not entertain fear.\' महेन्द्र name of a mountain. धैर्यमाधिषत 'their heart stook courage'.

LESSON XXX:

P. 220. 1. 11. नरपतिप्रबोधनार्थं i.e. to turn the eyes of the Princes which were fixed upon the king, to the Chandala girl who was being ushered in.

---11. 18-19. अनाश्रवासीत् 'did not mind it', turned a deaf ear. समगिरेतां 'pledged their word', 'vowed.'

P. 221. 1. 1. प्रतिविधाय तिष्ठासु 'having adopted, measures against the possible schemes of the king.'

---11. 3-4. वर्तयते 'maintains himself', lives on elephants killed\' by himself. 1. 4. 'A great person, who, by his prowess, humbles the world, does not forsooth wish for his own sustenance from others.'

314

P. 211.11. 6-7. अस्तसंख्यं 'so as to be beyond calculation', in countless numbers. अत्र 'in this battle.'

---1. 9. The idea is that a warrior, having recourse to mild or soft means (such as forgiveness) should accomplish his object, just &s a lamp sucks oil by means of the soft wick which intervenes, hut, for which the flame would be at once extinguished.

---1. 11-12. शक्ति 'strength'; had 'the three regal powers\' षड्गुण्यं 'the six expedients\' अंगानि 'limbs' and 'component members of a state.'

---1. 16. मा कस्यचिदुपस्कृथाः 'do not prepare (for me) any articles of food' such as condiment, spices, etc. (दृष‍यपेयभोज्यादिकं किमपि मा कुरु).

P. 222.1 2. वदमानः 'shining forth' (भासमानः)

---11. 4-5. व्यवहर्तुमभियोक्ष्यते 'will endeavour to go to a court of law.' लौपीनावशेषं etc. 'reduce him to absolute indigence.'

---1. 9. 'He with his (left) arm (always) raised up, lifts his right arm in this direction conformably to greet me'.

---11. 12-13. 'He, void of pride, always shows (to the world) his servants, as if they were his dear friends, treats his friends with a respect common to his nearest relations, and his relations as if they were vested with important authority.'

---11. 16-17. कृतपूर्वसंविद् &c. 'who had previously formed a plot for the accomplishment of their scheme.' समयोपलभ्यं 'to be 'got at the time' of the departure of Aja.

---11. 18-19. Said by Arjuna to Siva. संविदामीष 'lord of faculties.

1.19. विरोध्य etc. 'Of those who, through folly, become hostile, but afterwards become submissive.'

---11. 21-22. शान्तिमधिकृत्य asked the preceptor 'with reference to some expiatory rite for averting the evil.' स्वंतं 'resulting in good. '

---11. 25-26. भूपति 'the Chedi king' 1. 26'It is not probable that the lion (Krishna) will humbly crouch for fear of an attack'.

---11. 27-28. He had scarcely mastered the characters of the

315

alphabet written on the writing-tablet, when he enjoyed all the fruits of political instruction from association with men advanced in knowledge'.

P. 223. 11. 1-2. उदधिश्यामसीमां \'having the ocean for its dark boundary' i.e. as far as the very ocean. नगर etc. 'having arms as long as the bar of a city-gate, which is both long and massive, and hence indicative of great muscular strength.

---11. 7-14 Describe the Asoka garden of Ravana लतां नर्तयमानवत् 'as if making the creeper dance to the breeze.' संत्रस्ताः 'afraid of Ravana\'. नायासयन्त 'did not interfere with or affect' each coming round in due rotation. स्मरात् 'being love-smitten'.

---11. 15-16. The elephant, with his body tossed up, and hence imitating the lord of mountains about to dart up into the sky, made the driver get on himself, who placed his foot on the foot of the elephant slightly bent.

स दैवाधीनः कृतः,यद्भावितद्भवतु इत्युक्त्वा परित्यक्तः'he was *abandoned* to his fate.\'

तव निर्णये स्थास्यामि,तव निर्णयः प्रमाणं'I shall *abide* by (bow to) your decision.'प्रतीज्ञां-अभिसंधां-पालयति\''*abides* by his promise.\'

यथाशक्ति,यावच्छक्यं'to the best (utmost) of one's *ability*\', all that one can do, as far as possible.

बहुकौतुकःस देशः'the country *abounds* in curiosities.\'

पञ्चवर्षदेशीयः \'*about* five years old.मध्याह्नप्रायः-कल्पः समयः'it is*about*noon.'किं कर्तुमुद्यतोसि,किं कार्यव्यग्रोसि, किमारम्भस्त्वं'what are you *about*\'.

स सर्वेषां मूर्ध्नि तिष्ठति'he stands *above* (at the head of) all.'अदत्तावकाशो मत्सरस्य \'*above*envy.'

सा दारुणा प्रतिज्ञा लोके प्रकाशतां गता-प्रकाशीभूता'the dreadful vow became known *abroad*'

शून्यमनस्क, शून्यहृदय, हृदयेनासन्निहित, विगतचेतन'*absent-minded*.'

कृतमेतादृशेन असङ्गतेनप्रलापेन 'do not talk so *absurdly.*'

मनोरथानामगतिर्न विद्यते'nothing is *inacccessible* to desire.'

मरणंप्रकृतिः विकृतिर्जीवितमुच्यते'death is *nature*, life is but an*accident*.'

भावमनुप्रविश्'*accommodate* oneself to the will of.'

एकचित्तिभूय'with one *accord*.'यदृच्छया,स्वयं,स्वेच्छातः'of one's own*accord*.'तद्वचनानुसारेण-अनुरोधेन'in *accardance* with his words.\'अनुज्येष्ठं'*according* to seniority.'

राजेति का मात्रा-गणना मम 'of what *account* (consideration) is a king to me' (I defy him).
